    };
    var shopSwiper = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(swiper));
    var bannerSwiper = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(swiper));
    bannerSwiper.slidesPerView = 1;
    bannerSwiper.spaceBetween = 0;
    bannerSwiper.loop = true;
    bannerSwiper.autoplay = {
        delay: 3000
    };
    bannerSwiper.pagination = {
        el: '.swiper-pagination',
    };

    if ($(window).width() <= 600){
        swiper.slidesPerView = 2;
        shopSwiper.slidesPerView = 2;
    }

    $('#pills-profile-tab').on('shown.bs.tab', function (e) {
        new Swiper ('.special-swiper', swiper);
    });

    $(document).ready(function () {
        new Swiper ('.list-product-swiper', swiper);
        new Swiper ('.shop-swiper', shopSwiper);
        new Swiper ('.banner-swiper', bannerSwiper);
    })
</script>

            if (!sessionStorage.getItem('ignore-suggest')) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: window.location.origin + '/suggest-install-app',
                    type: 'get'
                }).done((data) => {
                    if (data === 'ios'){
                        $.confirm({
                            theme: 'supervan',
                            title: '',
                            content: `<div class="mb-4">Tải ứng dụng Vshop để sử dụng nhiều chức năng hơn</div><a href=""><img src="${window.location.origin}/courseselling/images/demo_page/applestore.png" alt=""></a>`,
                            buttons: {
                                'Để sau': function () {
                                    sessionStorage.setItem('ignore-suggest', 1);
                                },
                            }
                        });
                    }else if(data === 'android'){
                        $.confirm({
                            theme: 'supervan',
                            title: '',
                            content: `<div class="mb-4">Tải ứng dụng Vshop để sử dụng nhiều chức năng hơn</div><a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.vshop"><img src="${window.location.origin}/courseselling/images/demo_page/chplay.png" alt="">`,
                            buttons: {
                                'Để sau': function () {
                                    sessionStorage.setItem('ignore-suggest', 1);
                                },
                            }
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
        </script>
